25/09/21, 8:09â€¯pm - +91 70558 68288: The Life Member Affinity Group of the IEEE Bangalore Section is please to announce the following Webinar.                    
 Topic: *Graduates from Institutions are often criticised for not being ready for Industry; are Industries ready for Graduates of Institutions*?

Speaker: *Prof S. Sadagopan*

Date and Time: Tuesday, September 28, 2021; 6.00 PM - 7.30 PM.

*Meeting link*: https://ieeemeetings.webex.com/ieeemeetings/j.php?MTID=m86025391f7203ac387be4e3e509422a2
Meeting number:  2537 813 2603
Password: 5zkYmMBcK99                                                                                                                                                   Prof.   Lawrence Jenkins
Chairman       
                                                                                                                                                       *Speaker Profile*: 
*Prof Sadagopan* was the first Director of IIIT-Bangalore from 1999 to
2021. Earlier he taught at IIT Kanpur and IIM Bangalore. He did his Undergraduate Degree
(BE Hons) for College of Engineering, Guindy (India) and his Postgraduate Degrees (MS and
PhD) from Purdue University (USA) Currently he Chairs the Vision Group on Higher
Education and UVCE Modernization Committee; he is a Member of the Vision Group on IT      
                                     *ABSTRACT*: It has become fashionable in the last decade, particularly for captains of IT
industry to be very critical of engineering college graduates (the bulk of their recruitment
pool) stating that only a low percentage (as low as 5-10%) are ready for employment. They
often suggest â€œremedial measuresâ€ to be taken â€œto bridge the gapâ€ with help from industry
professionals. Why such a clamour particularly from Indian IT services companies alone?
Why increasingly now? Industry taking interest to improve engineering education is
welcome, but there must be soul searching on the other side too! This talk will raise some
interesting questions from the side of academia.

       With same thought, AI & ML CLUB is organizing a DEBATE COMPETITION on "How can Big Data become more useful and How do Business create better Analytical Models"as per schedule given below:- 

Date: 10th JUNE 2022 
Day: Friday 
Time: 3:30 pm
Venue: LAB 3

About the topic- 
Big data: It refers to data sets that are too large or complex in volume, variety to be dealt with by traditional data-processing application software.

Analytical Models: These are used to answer a specific question or make specific design decision for addressing different aspects of the system, such as its performance, reliability, or mass properties.

Rules and regulations: 
1) The maximum time will be 2 mins for each participant.
2) There will be 1 min time for Cross question round.
3) Evaluation will be based on Clarity, Content, Confidence, Originality and Presentation.
4) There is no language barrier.
5) The decision of Judges will be final.
